style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
*Taishõ Shinshû Daizõkyõ*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">大正新修大藏經</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">大正新修大蔵経</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA">)</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>6</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
*Leng‑chia Shih-tzu Chi*</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (<span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">*Ryõga Shijiki*</span><span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">楞伽師資記</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>7</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
*Cheng-tao-ko*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:JA">, </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Shõdõka*</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">證道歌</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">証道歌</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>8</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
mso-fareast-language:JA">永<span
style="color:black">嘉玄覺</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>9</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
*Ch'an-men Mi-yao <span
style="color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">Chüeh</span>*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(*Zenmon Hiyõketsu*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
mso-fareast-language:JA">禪門秘要決</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>10</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black"> *Sui-chao San-tsu* </span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(*Zuichõ Sanso Shinjinmei*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
mso-fareast-language:JA">隨朝三祖信心銘</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><img src="img/image008.jpg" width="83" height="32" /></span>

<span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**The
*Hsin-hsin Ming***</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
title of the *Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> may be
explained in the following way:</span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">信</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Hsin**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> means
"belief" or "faith." This is not the faith in the ordinary sense, it is
a belief that comes from firsthand experience, a faith which arise out
of supreme knowledge and wisdom of enlightenment. This "believing" is an
affirmation that all existence or reality is essentially the Buddha
mind, which is our true nature. *Hsin*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is the
conviction that at the bottom of all phenomena lies the One Mind, the
Buddha mind, which is one with our real nature, the
Buddha-nature.</span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">心</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Hsin**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
literally means "heart." It means mind, not the deluded mind of the
ignorant but the Buddha-mind. *Hsin*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is the
mind that merge with the all-encompassing One Mind.</span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">銘</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Ming**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
literally means "inscription." It means <span
style="color:black">written expression or </span>record.
*Ming*</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> also means <span
style="color:black">warnings or admonitions.</span></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Hsin-hsin
Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is one
of the earliest and most influential Zen writings. It is usually
referred to as the first Zen poem. It consists of 146 unrhymed
four-character</span><span style="font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><sup>1</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
verses</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>2</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(lines), total 584 characters</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><sup>3</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. The
*Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> was
composed in *shih*</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>4</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> form.
*Shih*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> was
the principal poetic form in use in the early period, it is first used
in the *Book of Odes*</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><sup>5</sup></span><span
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(*Shih-ching*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">,
*Shikyõ*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">). Like
the early *shih*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, the
*Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
consists of lines that are 4-characters in length, but contrary to most
*shih*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, no
end rhyme is employed in the poem.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>As a characteristic of *shih*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, one
line usually constitutes a single syntactical unit. Since one character
represents one syllable, and since classical Chinese is basically
monosyllabic, this means that there are usually four words to a line.
Lines tend to be end-stopped, with few run-on lines, so that the efffect
is of a series of brief and compact utterances.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>This concise form of four characters a line is
shorter than the general run of Chinese verse, which usually has five or
seven characters per line. Economy, even starkness of expression is a
characteristic of the *Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. It is
more of a verse than poetry and its brevity is one of the peculiar
characteristics of this famous work. Its contents is closer to the
Buddhist *sûtra*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">s than
poems. In fact, the *Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> can be
regarded as a *sûtra*</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. Many verses are like a short
Zen saying and therefore can be taken as if they are a single-sentence
Zen maxim. The original text was not divided in stanzas. Some
translators divided the poem in different ways, with or without adding
numbers to them.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>The *Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> has an
important place In Ch'an Buddhist tradition. The poem has been very
influential in Zen circles and many important commentaries were written
on it. The opening stanza, "The best way is not difficult. It only
excludes picking and choosing," is quoted by many Zen masters as well as
in the classical Zen works such as the *Blue Cliff Records*</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>6</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. Along
with the following influential poems, it is considered as a poem which
reveals the essence of Zen philosophy:</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**1.**</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Song
of Realizing the Way</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>*Cheng-tao-ko*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA"> (</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Shõdõka*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">,
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">證道歌</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>(variant title </span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">証道歌</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>by Ch'an </span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">master
</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Yung-chieh
Hsüan-chüeh*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (*Yõka
Genkaku*</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, 655-713 </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">永<span
style="color:black">嘉玄覺</span></span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**2.**</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Harmony of Difference and Sameness</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span><span
style="color:black">*Ts'an-t'ung-ch'i*</span><span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA"> (</span><span
style="color:black">*Sandõkai*</span><span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:
13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">參同契</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>by Ch'an </span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">master
*Shih-t'ou Hsi-ch'ien*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black"> (*Sekitõ Kisen*</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">, 700-790
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">石頭希遷</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">)</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**3.**</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Song
of Precious Mirror Samadhi<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span><span
style="color:black">*Pao-ching San-mei-ko*</span><span
style="color:black"> (*Hõkyõ Zanmaika*</span><span style="color:black">
</span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">寶鏡三昧歌</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>by </span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA">Ch'an </span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black">master *Tung-shan Liang-chieh*</span><span
style="font-size:
13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> (*Tõsan
Ryõkai*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black">, 807-869 </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">洞山良价</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**4.**</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Mind
Inscription</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>*Hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(*Shinmei*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">心銘</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:JA">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>by Ch'an </span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">master
</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Niu‑t'ou
Fa-jung*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (<span
style="color:black">*Gozu Hõ<span style="mso-fareast-language:
JA">yû</span>*</span><span style="color:black">, 594-657
</span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">牛頭法</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">融</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)<span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**5.**</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Mind
King Inscription</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>*Hsin-wang Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(*Shinnõmei*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">心王銘</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:JA">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span><span style="mso-fareast-language:
JA">by Ch'an </span><span style="color:black">master
*Fu-hsi*</span><span style="color:black"> (*Fukyû*</span><span
style="color:black">, ?-569 </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">傅翕</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">)</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
title of the work bears resemblance to three previously composed
poems:</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**1.**</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Mind
King Inscription</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>*Hsin-wang Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(*Shinnõmei*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">心王銘</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:JA">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span><span style="mso-fareast-language:
JA">by Ch'an </span><span style="color:black">master
*Fu-hsi*</span><span style="color:black"> (*Fukyû*</span><span
style="color:black">, ?-569 </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">傅翕</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**2.**</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Inscription of Stopping the Mind</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span><span style="mso-fareast-language:
JA">*Hsi-hsin Ming*</span><span style="mso-fareast-language:JA">
(*Sokushinmei*</span><span style="mso-fareast-language:JA">
</span></span><span lang="JA" style="font-size:
13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">息心銘</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>by *Chou*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
dynasty (1050-256 <span class="smallcaps">b.c.</span>) Ch'an master
*Wang-ming*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> <span
style="mso-fareast-language:
JA">(*Bõmei*</span><span style="mso-fareast-language:JA">
</span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">亡名</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:JA">)</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**3.**</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Enlightenment-Mind Inscription</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-TW"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>*Wu-hsin
Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW"> (*Goshinmei*</span><span style="font-size:
13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">悟心銘</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-TW"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span>by Elder
*Yüan-yin*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-TW"> (*Yüan-yin Lao-jen*</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">;
*Gen'on Rõnin*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">元音老人</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Another
important Ch'an poem Mind Inscription (*Hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">; *Shinmei*</span><span
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">心銘</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA">)</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, bears
a similar title and it is influenced by the *Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. This
poem <span style="mso-fareast-language:JA">attributed to Ch'an
</span><span style="color:black">master </span>*Niu‑t'ou
Fa-jung*</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>7</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (<span
style="color:black">*Gozu Hõ<span style="mso-fareast-language:
JA">yû</span>*</span>) <span style="color:black">has many points in
common with the </span>*Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, their <span
style="color:black">contents as well as styles are
similar.</span></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>A unique aspect of the *Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is the
particular Taoist concepts it contains, the poem, therefore, blends
together Buddhist and Taoist teachings. Words of Taoist origin such as
non‑action (*wu‑wei*</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><sup>8</sup></span><span
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">), no‑mind
(*wu‑hsin*</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>9</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">),
one‑mind (*i-hsin*</span><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><sup>10</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">),
spontaneity (*tzu‑jan*</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>11</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">),
vacuity (*hsü*</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><sup>12</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">), and
deep meaning (*hsüan-chih*</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>13</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)
clearly shows the profound influence that Taoism had on Zen.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Notes**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>1</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Four-character (four-word)
(*ssu-yen*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">四言</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>2</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Verse (*kou*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">句</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>3</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Character (*tzu*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">字</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)<span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>4</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>*Shih*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">詩</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>5</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>*Shih-ching*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(*Shikyõ*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">詩經</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:JA"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  
</span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">詩経</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>6</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Case 57, *Pi-yen Lu*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(*Hekiganroku*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">碧巖</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">錄</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">碧巌録</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)<span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>7</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>*Niu‑t'ou Fa-jung*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (<span
style="color:black">*Gozu Hõ<span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">yû</span>*</span><span
style="color:black">, 594-657 </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">牛頭法</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">融</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>8</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">爲</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>9</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">無心</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>10</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
mso-fareast-language:JA">一心</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>11</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
mso-fareast-language:JA">自然</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>12</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
mso-fareast-language:JA">虚</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><sup>13</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">玄旨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
following quotations contain further information on the *Hsin-hsin
Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">:</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">**Hakuyu
Taizan Maezumi Rõshi**</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">The
famous </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Hsin
hsin ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (Jap:
*Shin jin mei*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">) is
known as the first Zen poem. It <span style="color:black">consists of
146 four-word lines, directly and vividly expressing the Zen spirit in a
simple, compact form. An outstanding characteristic of the poem is that
it is written in genuine Chinese without using any Sanskrit or Pali
Buddhist terms.</span></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span>The main themes expressed in the
*Hsin hsin ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
derive from *Two Entries and Four Acts*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">, one of the few
authentic writings of the great Zen Patriarch Bodhidharma, who brought
Buddhism from India to China in the sixth century. The roots of
Bodhidharma's work can be traced to the *Vimalakirtinirdesa
Sutra*</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">, written sometime
before the third century <span class="smallcaps">c.e.</span> in India.
Even though authorship of the </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Hsin
hsin ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is
traditionally attributed to the Third Patriarch, Chien-chih Seng-ts'an
(Jap: *Kanchi Sosan*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">), the
idioms employed in the poem have caused some scholars to place the date
of its composition in a later year.</span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\[. . .\]</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>The title *Hsin hsin ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is
translated as *Verses on the Faith Mind*</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. The title of a poem is
sometimes likened to the forehead, which expresses a person's unique
characteristics. In *Hsin hsin ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">,
*hsin*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is
generally understood as "faith." However, the word is also used in a
different sense in the <span style="color:black">context of the verses,
as, for example, at the very end:</span></span>

<span
style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*Hsin hsin pu erh*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA">信心不二</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>Faith mind are not two</span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*Pu erh hsin hsin*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">       </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA">不二信心</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>Nondual faith mind</span>

<span
style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
translator renders these lines as:</span>

<span
style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*To live in this faith is the road to
nonduality*</span><span style="font-size:
13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*because the nondual is one with the trusting
mind.*</span><span style="font-size:
13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">In
this context, *faith*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black"> does not have the usual meaning of "having faith in
something," but rather that faith is the very *fact*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
of existence or reality itself. Dogen Zenji says, "Without attaining
Buddhahood, the faith won't manifest. Where the faith manifests, Buddhas
and </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Patriarchs
<span style="color:black">manifest" (*Shobogenzo*</span><span
style="color:black">). The *Nirvana Sutra*</span><span
style="color:black"> says, "Great faith is no other than Buddha nature."
Kozan Garyu says that "one thousand seven hundred koans are all together
the expression of this mind."</span></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span>The word *ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black"> means "written expression" and also "warnings or
admonitions," hence the title means "the verbal expression of the fact
that the very nature of existence and of all the phenomenal world are no
other than the faith mind." The </span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Hsin hsin ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
declares:</span>

<span
style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*Although all dualities come from the
one*</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*Do not be attached even to this One.*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span
style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">That
is to say, at the bottom of the two there is one and at the bottom of
one there is zero. And that zero is "just this," the unborn one Mind,
which is the faith mind.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span>From the time of its composition
up to the present day, the </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Hsin
hsin ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> has
been published and translated repeatedly by various scholars and
appreciated by different Chinese and Japanese masters, who have written
numerous commentaries on it. The masters' frequent references to the
poem have authenticated it as a genuine expression of the spirit of
Zen.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>In the Sung dynasty, the verse *Hsin hsin ming
nien-ku*</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> of Chen-hsieh Ch'ing-liao
(Jap: Shinketsu Seiryo, 1088-1151) was the first major commentary. Two
centuries later, in the Yuan dynasty, Chung-feng Ming-pen (Jap: Chuho
Myohun, 1263-1323) commented on the *Hsin hsin ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. In
1667, during the Ming dynasty, Wei-lin (Jap: I Rin) wrote *Hsin hsin
ming chu-yu*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (Jap:
*Jakugo*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">).</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>The founder of the Japanese Soto School, Dogen Zenji
(1200-1253), quoted a number of passages from the *Hsin hsin
ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> in his
*Eihei-koroku*</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, written in Chinese. In 1303, Keizan
Zenji, the cofounder of the Japanese Soto School, wrote the most famous
Japanese commentaries on the verse, known as the *Hsin hsin ming
nentei*</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> ("*Teisho*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> on the
*Hsin hsin ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">). In
1781, during the Edo period, Kozan Garyu wrote a commentary, the *Hsin
hsin ming yatosui*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, which
also contains Chen-hsieh Ch'ing-liao's verse and Keizan's
*Nentei*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">.
Rinzai master Isshi Benshu (1608-1646) also wrote a major commentary in
Japanese entitled the *Hsin hsin ming benchu*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>In modern times, several Japanese commentaries have
been written. Among the most famous are the commentaries by Kodo Sawaki
Roshi on Keizan Zenji's *Hsin hsin ming nentei*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> and by
Kodo Akino Roshi on Kozan Garyu's *Hsin hsin ming yatosui*</span><span
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. In addition, Ian
Kishizawa Roshi has written the *Hsin hsin ming kattoshu*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. D.T. Suzuki also gave
concise, pithy comments on the *Hsin hsin ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. The most recent commentary was written by
Koun Yamada Roshi. <span style="color:black">(*The Eye That Never
Sleeps*</span><span style="color:black"> xv-xviii)</span></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Thomas
Cleary**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">"Huike's
successor Sengcan, is traditionally credited with authorship of 'The
Trusting Heart,' one of the earliest and most enduringly popular works
on Zen. Quotations from this favorite work appear throughout later Zen
literature. Generally speaking, it is a guide to Zen meditation, but the
unifying theme is mental balance. Many of the Zen instructions
translated in the present volume are very much in the spirit of this
early Zen classic." (*Zen Essence*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
93)</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Heinrich
Dumoulin**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"a poem
attributed to the Third Patriarch, Seng-ts'an (d. 606), 'Words Inscribed
on the Believing Mind.' Part of the poem reads: 'When the one mind does
not arise, the myriad things (*dharma*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">) are
no obstacle./When there is no obstacle, no thing appears./And when no
thing appears, there is no mind.' As D.T. Suzuki makes clear in his
English paraphrase, these verses should not be understood in a
nihilistic sense. The key idea of the poem is the unity of nondualistic
reality. For the enlightened mind, all duality is overcome."</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA">(*Zen Buddhism: A History, Japan*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:JA">
280)</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Christmas
Humphreys**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Here,
then, to conclude, is an extract from the glorius poem of the third
Chinese Patriarch Seng-ts'an which he called 'On Trust in the Heart'. It
may be asked why, as it seems the most simple, it is put at the end of
so much harder reading. The answer is that although it is simple it is
at the same time enormously profound, and until it is realized that
these are not moral maxims for the class-room, but fragments from a vast
and deep experience, the quintessence of all the teaching that has gone
before, they will not be appreciated at their true value." (*Zen – A Way
of Life*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
127)</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Author
Unknown**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Suzuki
sensei's fine translation of Seng-ts'an's 'Hsin-hsin-ming' ('On
Believing in Mind,' pages 76-82), the very first verse treatise on Zen –
which in the original Chinese takes up just two thirds of a page in the
more than 100,000 pages of 'Taisho' – a text which embodies the
quintessence of Zen and that deserves to be far better known.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">(From a
book review of *Manual of Zen Buddhism*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> by
D.T. Suzuki)</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

original text of the *Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span

<span style="font-size:16.0pt;

mso-fareast-language:JA">　不一無忘一無無不正不動歸萬一良豈愚勿昏體轉寧元境萬紛唯勝無從寧泯所徒莫洞</span><span

<span style="font-size:16.0pt;

mso-fareast-language:JA">　二切即絶念不他勞信存止復法時由非人惡</span><span

JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">　信即是境萬包無心調軌無自一放</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">斟<span
lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">大自六不去轉偏一能無失息前不背一自不念順明</span></span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">　心一有界年容自力直則止然如卻</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">酌<span
lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">錯縛塵好住遲黨空</span></span><span
lang="ZH-TW"

font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">極動</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">観</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">異非</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">辺</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">心</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray">為</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">乘</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;mso-fareast-language:JA">真</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">然疑</span><span style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray">麁</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">段滅生非</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;mso-fareast-language:
JA">真</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">照慮有</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">辺懐</span><span lang="JA" style="font-size:
16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">捨旨前愛</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">     </span><span style="mso-tab-count:
1">     </span><span
lang="JA">　不一無忘一無無不正不動</span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">帰万</span><span lang="JA" style="font-size:
16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一良豈愚勿昏</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">体転</span><span lang="JA" style="font-size:
16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">寧元境萬紛唯勝無</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">従</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">寧泯所徒莫洞</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">     </span><span style="mso-tab-count:
1">     </span><span lang="JA">　二切即絶念不他</span></span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">労</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">信存止復法時由非人</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">悪</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">沈無急有是逐法然須</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">却処</span><span lang="JA" style="font-size:
16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">空知然以</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">労</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">存然</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">     </span><span style="mso-tab-count:
1">     </span><span lang="JA">　信即是境</span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">万</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">包無心調軌無自一放</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">斟<span
lang="JA" style="mso-fareast-language:JA">大自六不去</span></span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">転</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">偏一能無失息前不背一自不念順明</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">     </span><span style="mso-tab-count:
1">     </span><span
lang="JA">　心一有界年容自力直則止然如</span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">却</span><span style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">酌<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">錯縛塵好住</span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">遅党</span><span lang="JA" style="font-size:
16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">空沈咎心見空通空種</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">尽</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">如</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">静</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">逆白</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Translation
of the Text**</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Translated
by Prof. Dusan Pajin of Belgrade University, Yugoslavia</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<td style="text-align: left;" width="434" height="758" data-valign="top" data-bgcolor="white" style="vertical-align: top; background: white"><span style="position:absolute;left:0pt;z-index:29"> </span>

<tr class="odd">
<td><div class="shape" v:shape="_x0000_s1061" style="padding:3.6pt 7.2pt 3.6pt 7.2pt">
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:18.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">       </span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:18.0pt;
    font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong>F</strong></span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;
    font-family:Arial;color:white"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong>1</strong></span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong></strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">唯嫌揀擇</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>it only excludes picking and choosing.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">洞然明白</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>it will enlighten itself.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">天地懸隔</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>and heaven and earth are set apart.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">莫存順逆</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>do not be for or against.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">是爲心病</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>makes the mind sick.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">徒勞念靜</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>it is useless to quiet thoughts.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">無欠無餘</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>with nothing lacking, nothing in excess.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">所以不如</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>there is no suchness.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong>1</strong></span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong></strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">勿住空忍</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>do not dwell in emptiness.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">泯然自盡</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>everything will stop by itself.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">止更彌動</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>and rest will move you again.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">寧知一種</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>how will you know oneness?</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">二處失功</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>you will miss in two ways.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">從空背空</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>following emptiness you are always behind it.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">轉不相應</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>the more you will go astray.</strong> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">無處不通</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p> </p>
</div></td>
</tr>

 </td>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial"><span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                   
</span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:20.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">信心銘</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
Arial"></span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                   
</span>Faith-Mind Inscription**</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"><span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Arial">**1**</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Arial"></span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
5">                                    </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">至道無難</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>The best way is not
difficult**</span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
2">              </span><span
style="mso-tab-count:3">                      </span></span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">但莫憎愛</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Once you stop loving
and hating**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
5">                                    </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">毫釐有差</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Depart for a
hairbreadth**</span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
5">                                    </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">欲得現前</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>If you want it to
appear**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<td><div class="shape" v:shape="_x0000_s1062" style="padding:3.6pt 7.2pt 3.6pt 7.2pt">
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>and there is nothing you cannot understand.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">隨照失宗</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>following the outcome you lose the source.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">勝卻前空</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>and surpass the emptiness of things.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">皆由妄見</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>all have their cause in ignorance.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong>1</strong></span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong></strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">唯須息見</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>only abstain from views.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">慎勿追尋</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>be careful not to pursue them.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">紛然失心</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>and mind is lost in confusion.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">一亦莫守</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>however, do not even maintain the one.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">萬法無咎</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>then everything is without blame.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">不生不心</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>no arising, no mind.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">境逐能沈</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>the object is expelled when the subject sinks.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">能由境能</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>the subject is related to the object.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">元是一空</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>their origin is one emptiness.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">齊含萬象</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>evenly containing innumerable forms.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong>1</strong></span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong></strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">寧有偏黨</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>and you will not be for or against.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">無易無難</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>neither easy nor difficult.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">轉急轉遲</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>now in haste, then too late.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
    JA">必<span style="color:black">入邪路</span></span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p> </p>
</div></td>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Changes that go on
in emptiness**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Do not seek the

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;

mso-fareast-language:JA">二見不住</span><span

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span><span
style="mso-spacerun:
yes">  </span>Do not dwell in dual views,**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span

style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>The slightest trace
of right and wrong**</span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>One being is the

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>With one mind there

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>If you want to know
