<tr class="odd">
<td><div class="shape" v:shape="_x0000_s1063" style="padding:3.6pt 7.2pt 3.6pt 7.2pt">
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>and you will go astray.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">體無去住</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>essence neither goes nor abides.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">逍遙絶惱</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>and go free of troubles.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">昏沈不好</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>it darkens, sinks and spoils.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">何用疏親</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>of what use are strange and familiar?</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong>1</strong></span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong></strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">勿惡六塵</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>do not dislike the six sense‑objects.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">還同正覺</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>turns out equal to perfect awakenness.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">愚人自縛</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>the fool ties himself.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">妄自愛著</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>ignorance leads to preference.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">豈非大錯</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>is it not a great mistake?</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">悟無好惡</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>awakening negates liking and disliking.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">妄自斟酌</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>lead to absurd consideration.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">何勞把捉</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>why strive to grasp them?</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">一時放卻</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>away with this once for all.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">諸夢自除</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>all dreams stop by themselves.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong>1</strong></span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong></strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">萬法一如</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>all things are of one suchness.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">兀爾忘縁</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>resolutely neglect conditions.</strong></span></p>
<p> </p>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Arial">**<span

<span style="mso-ignore:vglayout;position:

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Fettered thinking

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>To weary the spirit
is not good;**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"><span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span></span><span

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>In following the One
vehicle**</span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
5">                                    </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">六塵不惡</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Not disliking the
six sense‑objects**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
5">                                    </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">智者無爲</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span

</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>All opposite

<td><div class="shape" v:shape="_x0000_s1064" style="padding:3.6pt 7.2pt 3.6pt 7.2pt">
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">歸復自然</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>you return again to spontaneity.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">不可方比</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>and nothing can be compared.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">動止無止</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>set rest in motion and there is no resting.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">一何有爾</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>how will one be for you?</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">不存軌則</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>and there is no principle or rule retained.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">所作倶息</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>which stops every action.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong>1</strong></span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:white"><strong></strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">正信調直</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>true faith is firm and harmonized.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">無可記憶</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>nothing to remember.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">不勞心力</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>power of the mind is not exerted.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">識情難測</span><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"> </span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>sense or feeling cannot fathom this.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">無他無自</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>there is neither other nor self.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">唯言不二</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>only express non‑duality.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">無不包容</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>nothing is left out.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">皆入此宗</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>all belong to this teaching.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">一念萬年</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>beyond a moment, or an eon.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">十方目前</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>everywhere in front of the eyes.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong> </strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">忘絶境界</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Arial"><strong>when boundaries are forgotten.</strong></span></p>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"> </span><span
style="mso-spacerun:
yes">     </span>Vacuous, enlightened, self‑illumined;**</span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
5">                                    </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">非思量處</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Thought is useless
here,**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span

5">                                    </span></span><span lang="JA"

mso-fareast-language:JA">眞如法界</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>In the real suchness
of the thing‑realm**</span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
5">                                    </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">要急相應</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Swiftly to accord
with that**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span

JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>In non-duality all
is equal,**</span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;

5">                                    </span></span><span lang="JA"

mso-fareast-language:JA">十方智者</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>The wise from all
directions**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
5">                                    </span></span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">宗非促延</span><span
style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>This teaching is not
urgent, or extensive,**</span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Not here, not
there,**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span></span><span

style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Arial"></span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;

style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Very small and large
are equal,**</span>

<span style="mso-ignore:vglayout;

<td><div class="shape" v:shape="_x0000_s1065" style="padding:3.6pt 7.2pt 3.6pt 7.2pt">
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">不見邊表</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>the limits cannot be seen.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">無即是有</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>with non‑being there is being.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">必不相守</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>do not hold on to it.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">一切即一</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>all is one.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">何慮不畢</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>worry not for finality.</strong></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"> </span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">不二信心</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>Non‑duality is faith in mind.</strong></span></p>
<p><span lang="JA" style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
    mso-fareast-language:JA">非去來今</span><span style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
    JA"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
    font-family:Arial"><strong>with no past, present, future.</strong></span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Arial"></span></p>
<p> </p>
</div></td>

are equal,**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>With being there is

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span

5">                                    </span></span><span lang="JA"

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>If not so –**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;

style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Merely with such
ability**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Faith in mind is
non‑dual.**</span>

<span style="font-size:18.0pt;
font-family:Arial;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:

style="font-size:18.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">言語道斷</span><span

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial">**<span
style="mso-tab-count:5">                                            
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span>Discourse here stops
–**</span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:Arial"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Chinese
and Japanese Transcriptions of the Text**</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">For
those who want to read the *Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> in Chinese or Japanese, Chinese and
Japanese transcriptions of the text are given here.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>Throughout this article, the *Tun-huang*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> manuscript version of the text is used. As
with most Chinese texts, there are minor differences between various
versions of the *Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">.
Variant lines and characters in the *Taishõ Daizõkyõ*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA"> (</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">vol.
48, No. 2010) version are indicated in this section.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**1**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> First
lines are Chinese readings (Wade-Giles transcription system).</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**2**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Second
lines are Chinese readings (Pinyin transcription system).</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**3**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Third
lines are Japanese readings (*kanbun yomi kudashi*</span><span
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">) according to Hepburn
transcription system (*Hebonshiki*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">).</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**4**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Fourth
lines are the translations of Dusan Pajin.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Variant
lines and characters are indicated on the right side.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When
pronunciations or English translations of the variant characters are the
same as the original characters, no variant pronunciations or
translations are given.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">      </span></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">**1**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"> </span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes"> </span></span><span lang="JA" style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">至道無難　唯嫌揀擇</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Chih-tao wu-nan. Wei
hsien chien-tse.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Zhi</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>4</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA">dao</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>2</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"> wu</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>2</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA">nan</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>2</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA">. Wei</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>2</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"> xian</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>2</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"> jian</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>3</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA">ze</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>2</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA">.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Shidõ bunan. Tada
kenjaku o kirau. (Shidõ bunan. Yui ken kenjaku.)</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>The best way is not
difficult. It only excludes picking and choosing.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">    </span></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">**3**</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">
</span><span

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span

chieh yu wang-chien.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Changes that go on in
emptiness all have their cause in ignorance.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Do not seek the true,
only abstain from views.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Niken ni jûsezu,

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Do not dwell in dual
views, be careful not to pursue them.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">纔有是非　紛然失心</span><span

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Wazuka ni zehi areba

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>The slightest trace of
right and wrong and mind is lost in confusion.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Ni wa itsu ni yotte

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>One being is the source
of the two, however, do not even maintain the one.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">**47**</span><span

yes"> </span></span><span lang="JA" style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一心不生　萬法無咎</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

wang-fa wu-chiu.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>With one mind there is
no arising, then everything is without blame.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

Pu-sheng, pu-hsin.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Toga nakereba hõ nashi.
Shõzezareba shin narazu.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>No blame, no things. No
arising, no mind.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>The subject follows
when the object ceases. The object is expelled when the subject

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>The object is related
to the subject. The subject is related to the object.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Ryõdan o shiran to
hosseba, moto kore ikkû.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>If you want to know
these two, their origin is one emptiness.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一空同兩　齊含萬象</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>I-kung liang t'ung,
ch'i han wan-hsiang.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Ikkû ryõ ni onaji,
hitoshiku banzõ o fukumu.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>In one emptiness both
are equal, evenly containing innumerable forms.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>The great way is
all‑embracing, neither easy nor difficult.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Shõken wa kogi su,
utata kyû nareba, utata ososhi.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Small views are
irresolute, full of doubt, now in haste, then too late.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA">?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Fukõ nareba shin o rõ
su. Nanzo soshin o mochiin?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>To weary the spirit is
not good. Of what use are strange and familiar?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;

Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">欲取一乘　勿惡六塵</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Ichijõ o toran to

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>In taking the One
vehicle, do not dislike the six sense‑objects.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span></span><span

Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">六塵不惡　還同正覺</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Liu-ch'en pu-eh, hai
t'ung cheng-chüeh.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Not disliking the six
sense‑objects turns out equal to perfect awakenness.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Chisha wa mui nari.
Gunin wa jibaku su.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>The wise performs
through non‑action. The fool ties himself.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">**81**</span><span

Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">法無異法　妄</span><span

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Fa wu-i fa, wang tzu

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Hõ ni ihõ nashi, midari
ni mizukara aijaku su.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Things are not
different, ignorance leads to preference.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">    </span></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">**83**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"> </span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes"> </span></span><span lang="JA" style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">將心用心　豈非大錯</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Chiang hsin yung hsin,
ch'i fei ta ts'o?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

kui-fu tzu-jan.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">so yu</span></p>

    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">itsu nanzo shõyû?<span style="color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span></p>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span

o zon suru koto nakare.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span

and there is no principle or rule retained.</span>

<span

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span

ichinen, bannen.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span

urgent, or extensive, beyond a moment, or an eon,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

</span><span

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;

<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>

    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">mamoru koto o sõ sezu<span style="color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span></p>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span

on to it.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Faith in mind is
non‑dual. Non‑duality is faith in mind.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span

</span><span

JA"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"> </span></span><span lang="JA"

mso-fareast-language:JA">言語道斷　非去來今</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span

chu lai chin.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Gongo dõdan – koraikon
ni arazu.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span>Discourse here stops –
with no past, present, future.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**An
Analysis of the *Hsin-hsin Ming***</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
following is an analysis of the *Hsin-hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> by Prof. Dusan Pajin of
Belgrade University, Yugoslavia. The article is published in the
following resources:</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">•
"On Faith in Mind". Journal of Oriental Studies, Vol. XXVI, No. 2, Hong
Kong 1988, pp. 270-288.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">•
"On Faith in Mind – Hsin Hsin Ming and Early Ch'an". Proceedings of the
XXII International Congress for Asian and North African</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span>Studies, Hamburg; in Zeitschrift der
Deutschen Morgenländischen Gesellschaft, Supplement IX, Stuttgart 1992,
p. 344</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">This article can
be also viewed in the following sites:</span>

<span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">https://dekart.f.bg.ac.yu/\~dpajin

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**On
Faith in Mind – Translation and Analysis of the *Hsin-hsin
Ming***</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">By
Prof. Dr. Dusan Pajin, Belgrade University, Yugoslavia</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Since
*Leng‑chia Shih‑tzu Chi*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>a</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> was
discovered,</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>1</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Seng‑ts'an's authorship of the *Hsin‑hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> has been doubted,
because of the remark that Seng-ts'an did not put any writings into
circulation. Ui</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>2</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> proposed that Seng-ts'an,
perhaps, only recited the text, otherwise written by someone else.
Nishitani and Yanagida</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>3</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> added
some further arguments, considering that the text was written in the
eighth century, two centuries after Seng‑ts'an. This was accepted as
valid by other authors.</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>4</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> \[</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>a</sup></span><span
style="font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
mso-fareast-language:JA">楞伽師資記</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\]</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Contributions
of the *Hsin-hsin Ming***</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Dumoulin</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>5</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> was
among the first to recognize that in many passages the composition of
*Hsin‑hsin Ming* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">is
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">akin to
the *Avatamsaka Sutra,* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">especially
the closing stanzas (30‑36).</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>Actually, there is some resemblance between the
concepts of one mind (stanza 123, oneness (stanzas 5,6,7) and one
vehicle (stanza 19) in *Hsin‑hsin Ming,* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">and
equivalent concepts developed in Hua‑yen</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>b</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. However, the obviously common subjects of
*Hsin‑hsin Ming* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">and
Hua‑yen are relativity and interpenetration of time and space dimensions
(in stanzas 32‑33), equality of things (st. 33) and the famous "one is
all, all is one"</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>c</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
principle (st. 35), which are explained later in detail (in "Analysis of
the Text" – related to sections VII and VIII of the *Hsin-hsin
Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">). On
such grounds we can conclude that this text should be – at least partly
– related also with the Hua‑yen tradition (i.e., not exclusively with
Ch'an). </span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\[</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>b</sup></span><span
style="font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
mso-fareast-language:JA">華嚴</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:JA"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  
</span></span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>c</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一即一切、一切即一</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\]</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>We can outline two significant contributions of the
*Hsin‑hsin ming* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">to the
overall tradition of Chinese Buddhism.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**a.<span
style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span>**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
first is "faith in mind", which could be considered as a "Ch'anist"
response to the Buddhism of faith (Pure Land</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> <sup>d</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">), since the object of faith is
not Amitabha</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>e</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, but
mind as a means of awakening. </span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\[</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>d</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">浄土</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span></span><span style="font-size:
11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>e</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">阿弥陀</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\]</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**b.<span
style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">   </span>**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
second contribution is the principle of oneness (*i‑chung*</span><span
style="font-size:
11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>f</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)*.*
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It is
particularly mentioned in stanzas 5, 6 and 7. Otherwise, it is the
running idea of the whole text, continually warning against various
dualities: liking‑disliking (stanzas 1, 19, 21), grasping‑rejecting (st.
3), conditions/form‑emptiness (st. 5, 14), motion‑rest (st. 6, 21, 26),
truth‑views (st. 10), right‑wrong (st. It, 23), things/dharmas‑mind (st.
123, subject‑object (st. 133), coarse‑fine (st. 15), strange‑familiar
(st. 18), sense‑objects/awakeness (st. 19), things/dharmas‑suchness (st.
24), profit-loss (st. 23) other‑self (st. 25, 30), moment‑eon (st. 32),
here‑there (st. 32), small‑large (st. 33), one‑all (st. 35). These
dualities should be refuted or transcended with the perspective of one
mind – in emptiness and real suchness. </span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\[</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>f</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一種</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\]</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Broadly
speaking, *Hsin‑hsin Ming*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is an
elegant exposition of *prajna* </span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">(principles), and *dhyana*
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">(practice).
With approximation, we can say that sections I, V, and VI mostly deal
with principles (oneness, one mind, emptiness, suchness), sections II.
III, and IV mostly expose practice, while sections VII, and VIII
describe the results of such practice, and applied principles.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Problems
of Translating**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In
translating ancient religious and philosophical texts, one of the major
problems is to decide – in case it is not a *terminus technicus per
se*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> –
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">whether
a certain word (in our case, a Chinese character) is used colloquially,
or as a *terminus technicus*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. On
such a decision sometimes depends not only the **appropriate
translation**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> of a
particular word, but the **proper understanding**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> of the whole passage, as well.
To decide, we should know the tradition of the text and have in mind the
context, as well as previous commentaries, if such exist (nevertheless,
these can also be misleading, since in many cases they are comments, not
for the sake of interpreting, but in order to give support and authority
of the tradition to the thoughts of their respective authors).</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>The second problem is that the translator uses a
language the words of which have the same ambiguity
(colloquial‑technical) as the original language, or a vocabulary which
(itself) lacks the necessary technical terms. This can be solved by
using capitals, italics, etc. Also, one of the solutions for translating
Chinese Buddhist texts was to use the Sanskrit terms as technical, in
the same manner as in European philosophy one would use Greek or Latin,
instead of native words, in order to convey the technical meaning and
avoid ambiguity.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>Meaning is developed through use. For example, for
"awakening" or "enlightenment" no one uses capitals; through lengthy use
it is supposed that these will not be misunderstood (that they will be
understood as technical terms in a Buddhist context, and not in
colloquial meaning). But some terms (One, Way, Void, Suchness) are still
written with capitals. For translations from Chinese it is still
customary to use Sanskrit equivalents to pinpoint the meaning, or when
the terms from European languages are not good enough. For example,
Chinese *fa*</span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>g</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is better translated with
Sanskrit *dharma,* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">than
with "things" (as was done in this translation – but, to use "dharma"
supposes that the reader is more familiar with Sanskrit, than with the
Chinese, which, for the average person is not the case). </span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\[</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>g</sup></span><span
style="font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
mso-fareast-language:JA">法</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\]</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>Wing‑tsit Chan remarked that "Without adequate tools
to help them, many translators have rendered technical terms in their
popular meanings".</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>6</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Fortunately, some sixty years ago, Soothill and Hodous,</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>7</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> filled the gap for Chinese Buddhist terms
with their dictionary. However, their dictionary was possible thanks to
the work done some 1500 years ago, by generations of Chinese Buddhists,
who translated Sanskrit Buddhist texts into Chinese, using and
standardizing certain Chinese characters as technical terms
(equivalents) for Sanskrit terms.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>In order to proceed with the analysis of the
*Hsin‑hsin Ming,* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">and its
general meaning in the context of Chinese Buddhism, particularly Ch'an,
we propose a new translation. Originally, the text, as presented in
*Taisho*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
(*Taisho shinshu daizokyo*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>h</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">) No.
2010, was not divided in stanzas. The translators, excepting Suzuki,
were faithful to this form. In the second version of his translation
Suzuki has added numbers to the stanzas, in which he grouped the lines
of the poem (his first translation, let it be remarked, omits four
verses of stanza 6).</span><span style="font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>10</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> In
order to make possible easy reference for the analysis we have also
divided the poem in stanzas, but this "versification" differs from
Suzuki's version. However, in the right hand row we have given the
numbers of his stanzas in brackets (for those who want to compare the
translations). For easy reference we also suggest a division of the text
into eight (principal) parts, notated with Roman numerals (I-VIII).
</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\[</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>h</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">大正新修大藏經</span><span
style="font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span><span
lang="JA">大正新修大蔵経</span></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\]</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Analysis
of the Text**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now we
shall proceed with the analysis of the text, section by section
(I‑VIII), explaining technical terms, their meaning in the context of
Chinese Buddhism, and the main ideas of the text. When necessary we
shall also reach for the wider context of Indian Buddhism, in order to
explain the history of certain concepts.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**I**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Hsin‑hsin
Ming* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">mentions
faith (*hsin*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>i</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">) in
its title and in the concluding stanza (36). We know that faith (Skt.
*sraddha*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">in
Buddhism is one of the five qualities for making progress on the path
(Skt. *marga*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">).
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Various
texts speak of faith in Buddha (*Tathagata*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>j</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">), the Buddhist doctrine
(*Dharma*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>k</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">), as
well as Buddhist community, or assembly (*Sangha*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>l</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">). In certain Mahayanic texts
(*Sukhavativyuha*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">,
*Mahayanasraddhotpada*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">,
*Amitayurdhyana*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">) faith
has been promoted as a principal quality, and an agent of salvation.
K.N. Jayatilleke</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>11</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> has
indicated three aspects of faith in early Buddhism: affective, conative
and cognitive. In later Buddhism a theistic aspect of faith is
introduced, and faith is redefined. Sakyamuni as a historical person is
enveloped by a deified transhistorical Buddha. The faith that Sakyamuni
attained at awakening, (which is – under certain conditions and precepts
– repeatable for other Buddhists), has been transformed into a faith
(related to worship and reverence) that salvation is based on a
transcendental, omnipotent, transhistorical principle (Adi-Buddha), and
bestowed to the faithful, with compassion, as grace from his emanations
(other Buddhas, and bodhisattvas). </span><span style="font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\[</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>i</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">信</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span></span><span style="font-size:
11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>j</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">如來</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun:
yes">   </span></span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>k</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">法</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span></span><span style="font-size:
11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>l</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">僧伽</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\]</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>With this background, "faith in mind"</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>m</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is an original contribution of
*Hsin‑hsin Ming.* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It
introduces the meditative aspect of faith, based on mind-doctrine
affirmed in Ch'an. To have "faith in mind" means to have faith that
awakening will follow when the mind "returns to the root (or
source)"</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>n</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> and
stops discriminating (realizes one-ness). It is based on a common
denominator present in all sects of Ch'an tradition: "Mind is the root
of the myriad phenomena... If you can completely comprehend mind, the
myriad practices are completed".</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>12</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\[</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>m</sup></span><span
style="font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
mso-fareast-language:JA">信心</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:JA"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  
</span></span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>n</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">歸根</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\]</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>In the first stanza of *Hsin‑hsin Ming* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">we encounter the refutation of dualities.
Perhaps, the author—whoever he was—was aware of the paradox, rather
common in Taoism and Ch'an, when he said that the best way is not
difficult, under the condition which is most difficult for humans: to
stop loving and hating, picking and choosing.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>The first four stanzas bear a definitely Taoist
influence (compare *Lao‑tzu*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, I).
They banish feelings and duality, connecting the way with vacuity
(*hsu*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>o</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">) and
deep meaning (*hsuan chih*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>p</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">). In
relation to vacuity (*hsu*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">) we
should emphasize the difference in meaning between this character in
Taoism and the meaning of emptiness (*k'ung*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>q</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">) in Buddhism. Lao‑tzu (Ch. II)
proposes the ideal of a "vacuous" (*hsu*</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">) heart for man, that
is, of peace and purity of mind, freedom from worry and egoism. To
maintain this vacuity (according to *Lao‑tzu*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, Ch. 15‑16) is to be open for
the *tao*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> and
its way, "open and broad, like a valley". It means to keep the
receptive, feminine aspect of mind, in order to be able to accord with
the *tao.* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Emptiness
(*k'ung*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">) will
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">be
explained later in relation to stanzas 5, 7, 9 and 14. </span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\[</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>o</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">虚</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span></span><span style="font-size:
11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>p</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:JA">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA">玄旨</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">   </span></span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>q</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">
</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">空</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\]</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>In the first line (st. 1) we decided to translate
*chih‑tao*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>r</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> as
"the best way". Blyth</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>13</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> has
suggested "great way" which is not wrong *per se*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, but
since in stanza 15 we already have *ta tao*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>s</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, which must be "great tao", it was
unreasonable to use the same word for different characters. In this
translation we have been—as far as possible—faithful to the principle
that the same character should be translated with the same word and
*vice versa*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> – a
different character with a different word. Other translators decided to
use "perfect way" as equivalent for *chih‑tao.* </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">This is
not wrong, but "perfect" also denotes something that has been brought to
the end, finished. However, speaking of the way, we have something that
has yet to be threaded. That is why we made an option for the "best
way". On the other hand we have reserved "perfect" as equivalent for
*cheng*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>t</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, which
appears in stanza 19. We understand that the "way" (which is spoken of
in the first four stanzas) is not the Taoist *tao*</span><span
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, but the way of
Buddhism (Skt. *marga*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">). With
stanza 4 we leave the Taoist meanings, since the "great
vacuity"</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>u</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, which
is a Taoist expression, is related to a peculiarly Buddhist term
("suchness"). In the fourth line of stanza 4 Waley missed the meaning of
*ju*</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>v</sup></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">. He
takes the colloquial meaning (so), instead of the technical, Buddhist
meaning – suchness, thatness (Skt. *tathata*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">). </span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\[</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><sup>r</sup></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span lang="JA"
style="font-family:
