<td><div class="shape" v:shape="_x0000_s1056" style="padding:3.6pt 7.2pt 3.6pt 7.2pt">
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><strong>On Believing in Mind</strong></span><span style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:6.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Except that it refuses to make <span style="color:gray"><strong>preferences</strong></span>;</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you <span style="color:gray"><strong>wish</strong></span> to see it <span style="color:gray"><strong>before your own eyes</strong></span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray"><strong>Have</strong></span><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> no <span style="color:gray"><strong>fixed thoughts</strong></span> either for or against it.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Peace of mind is disturbed <span style="color:gray">to no purpose</span>.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">Be</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> serene in the oneness of things,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:
    14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">And</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> [dualism] vanishes by itself.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The <span style="color:gray">denying</span> of reality <span style="color:gray">is the asserting of it</span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">And the asserting of emptiness is the denying of it</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span></p>
</div></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
 </td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Inscribed
On the Believing Mind**</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Translated by Daisetsu Teitarõ
Suzuki</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">至道無難</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The Perfect Way knows no
difficulties</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">唯嫌揀擇</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Except that it refuses to make
preference:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">但莫憎愛</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Only when freed from hate and
love,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">洞然明白</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>It reveals itself fully and without
disguise.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">毫釐有差</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>A tenth of an inch's
difference,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">天地懸隔</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>And heaven and earth are set
apart:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">欲得現前</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>If you want to see it
manifest,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">莫存順逆</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Take no thought either for or against
it.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">違順相爭</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>To set up what you like against what
you dislike –</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">是</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">爲心病</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span>This is the disease of the
mind:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不識玄旨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When the deep meaning \[of the Way\]
is not understood</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">徒勞念靜</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Peace of mind is disturbed and
nothing is gained.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">圓同太虚</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\[The
Way is\] perfect like unto vast space,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無欠無餘</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>With nothing wanting, nothing
superfluous:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">良由取捨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>It is indeed due to making
choice</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">所以不如</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>That its suchness is lost sight
of.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">莫逐有縁</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Pursue not the outer
entanglements,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">勿住空忍</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Dwell not in the inner void;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一種平懷</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When the mind rests serene in the
oneness of things,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">泯然自盡</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The dualism vanishes by
itself.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">止動歸止</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When you strive to gain quiescence by
stopping motion,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">止更彌動</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The quiescence thus gained is ever in
motion;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">唯滯兩邊</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>As long as you tarry in the
dualism,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">寧知一種</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>How can you realize oneness?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一種不通</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>And when oneness is not thoroughly
understood,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">兩處失功</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>In two ways loss is sustained
–</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">遣有沒有</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The denial of reality may lead to its
absolute negation,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">從空背空</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>While the upholding of the void may
result in contradicting itself.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">多言多慮</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Wordiness and intellection –</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">轉不相應</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The more with them the further astray
we go;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">絶言絶慮</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Away therefore with wordiness and
intellection,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無處不通</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>And there is no place where we cannot
pass freely.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">歸根得旨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When we return to the root, we gain
the meaning;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">隨照失宗</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When we pursue external objects, we
lose the reason.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">須臾返照</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The moment we are enlightened
within,</span>

<span style="mso-ignore:vglayout;position:
absolute;z-index:31;left:0px;margin-left:648px;margin-top:162px;width:362px;
height:638px"> </span>

<table data-cellpadding="0" data-cellspacing="0">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr class="odd">
<td style="text-align: left;" width="362" height="638" data-valign="top" data-bgcolor="white" style="vertical-align: top; background: white"><span style="position:absolute;left:0pt;z-index:28"> </span>
<table data-cellpadding="0" data-cellspacing="0" width="100%">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr class="odd">
<td><div class="shape" v:shape="_x0000_s1060" style="padding:3.6pt 7.2pt 3.6pt 7.2pt">
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">Abide</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> not with dualism,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Confusion ensues, and <span style="color:gray">Mind</span> is lost.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The two exist because of the <span style="color:gray">One</span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But hold not even to this <span style="color:gray">One</span>;</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When <span style="color:gray">a</span> mind is not disturbed,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:6.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">No offence <span style="color:gray">offered, and no ten thousand things</span>;</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">No disturbance going, and no mind set up to work:</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The subject is quieted <span style="color:gray">when</span> the object ceases,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The object ceases <span style="color:gray">when</span> the subject is quieted.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:8.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The subject is a subject for <span style="color:gray">the</span> object:</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:6.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Rests ultimately on <span style="color:gray">one Emptiness</span>.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In <span style="color:gray">one Emptiness</span> the two are <span style="color:gray">not distinguished</span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And each contains in itself all the ten thousand things</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:8.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The Great Way is calm and large-<span style="color:gray">hearted</span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">For it</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, nothing is easy, nothing is hard;</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:
    14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Clinging <span style="color:gray">is never kept</span> within bounds,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I---</span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:8.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">Quit it</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, and things <span style="color:gray">follow their own courses</span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">While the <span style="color:gray">Essence</span> neither departs nor abides.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p> </p>
</div></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
 </td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">勝卻前空</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>We go beyond the voidness of a world
confronting us.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">前空轉變</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Transformations going on in an empty
world which confronts us,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">皆由妄見</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Appear real all because of
Ignorance:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不用求眞</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Try not to seek after the
true,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">唯須息見</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Only cease to cherish
opinions.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">二見不住</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Tarry not with dualism,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">慎莫追尋</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Carefully avoid pursuing it;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">纔有是非</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>As soon as you have right and
wrong,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">紛然失心</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Confusion ensues, and mind is
lost.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">二由一有</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The two exist because of the
one,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一亦莫守</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>But hold not even to this one;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一心不生</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When the one mind is not
disturbed,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">萬法無咎</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The ten thousand things offer no
offence.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無咎無法</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When no offence is offered by them,
they are as if not existing;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不生不心</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When the mind is not disturbed, it is
as if there is no mind.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">能隨境滅</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The subject is quieted as the object
ceases,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">境逐能沈</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The object ceases as the subject is
quieted.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">境由能境</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The object is an object for the
subject,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">能由境能</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The subject is a subject for an
object:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">欲知兩段</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Know that the relativity of the
two</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">元是一空</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Rests ultimately on the oneness of
the void.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一空同兩</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>In the oneness of the void the two
are one,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">齊含萬象</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>And each of the two contains in
itself all the ten thousand things:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不見精</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">麁</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When no discrimination is made
between this and that,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">寧有偏黨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>How can a one-sided and prejudiced
view arise?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">大道體寛</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The Great Way is calm and
large-minded,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無易無難</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Nothing is easy, nothing is
hard:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">小見狐疑</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Small views are irresolute,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">轉急轉遲</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The more in haste the tardier they
go.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">執之失度</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Clinging never keeps itself within
bounds,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">必<span
style="color:black">入邪路</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>It is sure to go the wrong way:<span
style="mso-tab-count:3">                      </span></span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">放之自然</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Let go loose, and things are as they
may be,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">體無去住</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>While the essence neither departs nor
abides.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">任性合道</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Obey the nature of things, and you
are in concord with the Way,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">逍遙絶惱</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Calm and easy and free from
annoyance;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">繋念乖眞</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>But when your thoughts are tied, you
turn away from the truth,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">昏沈不好</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>They grow heavier and duller and are
not at all sound.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="mso-ignore:vglayout;position:
relative;z-index:32"><span style="left:0px;position:absolute;left:639px;
top:-9px;width:425px;height:722px"> </span></span>

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>

<tr class="odd">
<td style="text-align: left;" width="425" height="722" data-valign="top" data-bgcolor="white" style="vertical-align: top; background: white"><span style="position:absolute;left:0pt;z-index:25"> </span>
<table data-cellpadding="0" data-cellspacing="0" width="100%">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr class="odd">
<td><div class="shape" v:shape="_x0000_s1057" style="padding:3.6pt 7.2pt 3.6pt 7.2pt">
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When they are not sound, the <span style="color:gray">spirit</span> is troubled;</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">You <span style="color:gray">are then one</span> with <span style="color:gray">the</span> Enlightenment;</span><span style="font-size:
    14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:8.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Is this not the greatest of <span style="color:gray">all</span> self-contradictions?</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:2.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">The ignorant cherish the idea</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> of rest and unrest,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:8.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Are contrived <span style="color:gray">by the ignorant themselves</span>.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:8.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If the Mind retains its <span style="color:gray">absoluteness</span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The ten thousand things are of one <span style="color:gray">Suchness</span>.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:
    14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When the deep mystery of one <span style="color:gray">Suchness</span> is fathomed,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">We return to the origin and remain <span style="color:gray">where we ever have been</span>.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Movement stopped <span style="color:gray">and there</span> is no movement,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Rest set in motion <span style="color:gray">and there</span> is no rest;</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:8.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Oneness itself <span style="color:gray">abides not</span>.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">In</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> the Mind <span style="color:gray">harmonious</span> [with the Way] <span style="color:gray">we have</span> the principle of</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In which we find all <span style="color:gray">strivings quieted</span>;</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p> </p>
</div></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
 </td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不好勞神</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When they are not sound, the soul is
troubled;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">何用疏親</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>What is the use of being partial and
one-sided then?</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">欲取一乘</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>If you want to walk the course of the
One Vehicle,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">勿惡六塵</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Be not prejudiced against the six
sense-objects.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">六塵不惡</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When you are not prejudiced against
the six sense-objects,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">還同正覺</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes"> </span>You in turn identify yourself with
Enlightenment;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">智者無爲</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The wise are non-active,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">愚人自縛</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>While the ignorant bind themselves
up;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">法無異法</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>While in the Dharma itself there is
no individuation,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">妄</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">自愛著</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span>They ignorantly attach themselves to
particular objects.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">將心用心</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes"> </span>It is their own mind that creates
illusions –</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">豈非大錯</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Is this not the greatest of
self-contradictions?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">迷生寂亂</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Ignorance begets the dualism of rest
and unrest,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">悟無好惡</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The enlightened have no likes and
dislikes:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一切二邊</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>All forms of dualism</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">妄</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">自斟酌</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span>Are ignorantly contrived by the mind
itself.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">夢幻虚華</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>They are like unto visions and
flowers in the air:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">何勞把捉</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Why should we trouble ourselves to
take hold of them?</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">得失是非</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Gain and loss, right and wrong
–</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一時放卻</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Away with them once for all!</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">眼若不睡</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>If an eye never falls asleep,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">諸夢</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">自除</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span>All dreams will by themselves
cease:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">心若不異</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>If the mind retains its
oneness,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">萬法一如</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The ten thousand things are of one
suchness.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一如體玄</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When the deep mystery of one suchness
is fathomed,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">兀爾忘虚</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>All of a sudden we forget the
external entanglements:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">萬法齊觀</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When the ten thousand things are
viewed in their oneness,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">歸復自然</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>We return to the origin and remain
what we are.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">泯其所以</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Forget the wherefore of
things,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不可方比</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>And we attain to a state beyond
analogy:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">止動無動</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Movement stopped is no
movement,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">動止無止</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>And rest set in motion is no
rest.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">兩既不成</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When dualism does no more
obtain,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一何有爾</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Even oneness itself remains not as
such.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">究竟窮極</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The ultimate end of things where they
cannot go any further,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不存軌則</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Is not bound by rules and
measures:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">契心平等</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The mind in harmony \[with the Way\]
is the principle of identity<span style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span><span
style="mso-tab-count:10">                                                                                         
</span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">     </span></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">identity</span><span
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">所作倶息</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>In which we find all doings in a
quiescent state;</span>

<span style="mso-ignore:vglayout;
position:relative;z-index:33"><span style="left:0px;position:absolute;
left:639px;top:-3px;width:452px;height:731px"> </span></span>

<tr class="odd">
<td style="text-align: left;" width="452" height="731" data-valign="top" data-bgcolor="white" style="vertical-align: top; background: white"><span style="position:absolute;left:0pt;z-index:26"> </span>
<table data-cellpadding="0" data-cellspacing="0" width="100%">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr class="odd">
<td><div class="shape" v:shape="_x0000_s1058" style="padding:3.6pt 7.2pt 3.6pt 7.2pt">
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">Doubts and</span><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> irresolutions are completely done away with,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And the right faith is <span style="color:gray">straightened</span>;</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">There is</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> nothing <span style="color:gray">left behind</span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">There is</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> nothing <span style="color:gray">retained</span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:6.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">There is no <span style="color:gray">exertion</span>, no <span style="color:gray">waste</span> of energy</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In the higher realm of <span style="color:gray">true</span> Suchness</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">There is neither <span style="color:gray">"self"</span> nor <span style="color:gray">"other"</span>:</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When direct identification is <span style="color:gray">sought</span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:6.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In being <span style="color:gray">"not two"</span> all is the same,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">They all enter into this <span style="color:gray">Absolute Reason</span>.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">This <span style="color:gray"><strong>Absolute Reason</strong></span> is beyond quickening [time] and <span style="color:gray"><strong>extending</strong></span> [space],</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">For it</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> one instant is ten thousand years;</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:
    14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Whether <span style="color:gray">we see it or not</span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It is manifest everywhere <span style="color:gray">in all the ten quarters.</span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:
    14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:2.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Infinitely small <span style="color:gray">things are</span> as large as large <span style="color:gray">things</span> can be,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">For here no</span><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> external conditions <span style="color:gray">obtain</span>;</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Infinitely large <span style="color:gray">things are</span> as small as small <span style="color:gray">things</span> can be,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">For</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> objective limits are <span style="color:gray">here of no consideration</span>.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray"><em>What is</em></span><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is the same <span style="color:gray">as</span> what is not,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
    color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray"><em>What is</em></span><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> <em>not</em> </span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">is the same <span style="color:gray">as</span> what is:</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:6.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">Indeed, no tarrying there</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:
    14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:5.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">One in <span style="color:gray">All</span>,</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">All in <span style="color:gray">One</span> –</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:10.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">Where Mind and each</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> believing mind <span style="color:gray">are</span> not divided,</span><span style="font-size:
    14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And undivided <span style="color:gray">are each</span> believing mind <span style="color:gray">and Mind,</span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:6.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">For it is not of the past, <span style="color:gray">present, and future</span>.</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span></p>
<p> </p>
</div></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
 </td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">狐疑盡淨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Irresolutions are completely done
away with,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">正信調直</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>And the right faith is restored to
its native straightness;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一切不留</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Nothing is retained now,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無可記憶</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Nothing is to be memorized,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">虚明自照</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>All is void, lucid, and
self-illuminating,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不勞心力</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>There is no stain, no exertion, no
wasting of energy –</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">非思量處</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>This is where thinking never
attains,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">識情難測</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>This is where the imagination fails
to measure.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">眞如法界</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>In the higher realm of True
Suchness</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無他無自</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>There is neither 'other' nor
self':</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">要急相應</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When a direct identification is asked
for,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">唯言不二</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>We can only say, 'Not two.'</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不二皆同</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>In being not two all is the
same,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無不包容</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>All that is is comprehended in
it:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">十方智者</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The wise in the ten quarters,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">皆入此宗</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>They all enter into this absolute
faith.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">宗非促延</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>This absolute faith is beyond
quickening \[time\] and extension \[space\].</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一念萬年</span><span
