style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>One instant is ten thousand
years;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無在不在</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>No matter how things are conditioned,
whether with 'to be' or 'not to be',</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">十方目前</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>It is manifest everywhere before
you</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">極小同大</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The infinitely small is as large as
large can be,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">忘絶境界</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When external conditions are
forgotten;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">極大同小</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The infinitely large is as small as
small can be,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不見邊表</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When objective limits are put out of
sight.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">有即是無</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>What is is the same with what is
not,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無即是有</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>What is not is the same with what
is:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">若不如此</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Where this state of things fails to
obtain,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">必不相守</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Be sure not to tarry.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一即一切</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>One in all,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一切即一</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>All in one –</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">但能如是</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>If only this is realized;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">何慮不畢</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>No more worry about your not being
perfect!</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">信心不二</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The believing mind is not
divided,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不二信心</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>And undivided is the believing mind
–</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">言語道斷</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>This is where words fail,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">非去來今</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>For it is not of the past, future, or
present.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="mso-ignore:vglayout;
position:relative;z-index:34"><span style="left:0px;position:absolute;
left:639px;top:-12px;width:263px;height:38px"> </span></span>

<table data-cellpadding="0" data-cellspacing="0">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr class="odd">
<td style="text-align: left;" width="263" height="38" data-valign="top" data-bgcolor="white" style="vertical-align: top; background: white"><span style="position:absolute;
  left:0pt;z-index:27"> </span>
<table data-cellpadding="0" data-cellspacing="0" width="100%">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr class="odd">
<td><div class="shape" v:shape="_x0000_s1059" style="padding:3.6pt 7.2pt 3.6pt 7.2pt">
<p><span style="font-size:4.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:
    &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">(<em>Manual of Zen Buddhism</em></span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> 91-7)</span><span style="font-size:
    14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:white">I</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
    font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></p>
<p> </p>
</div></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
 </td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">(*Essays
in Zen Buddhism – First Series*</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> 196-201)</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Verses On the Faith
Mind**</span><span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Translated by Richard B.
Clarke</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">至道無難</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The Great Way is not difficult</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">唯嫌揀擇</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>for those who have no
preferences.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">但莫憎愛</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When love and hate are both
absent</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">洞然明白</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>everything becomes clear and
undisguised.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">毫釐有差</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Make the smallest distinction,
however</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">天地懸隔</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and heaven and earth are set
infinitely apart.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">欲得現前</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>If you wish to see the truth</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">莫存順逆</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>then hold no opinions for or against
anything.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">違順相爭</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>To set up what you like against what
you dislike</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">是</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">爲心病</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span>is the disease of the mind.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不識玄旨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When the deep meaning of things is
not understood</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">徒勞念靜</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>the mind's essential peace is
disturbed to no avail.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">圓同太虚</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The Way
is perfect like vast space</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無欠無餘</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>where nothing is lacking and nothing
is in excess.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">良由取捨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Indeed, it is due to our choosing to
accept or reject</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">所以不如</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>that we do not see the true nature of
things.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">莫逐有縁</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Live neither in the entanglements of
outer things,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">勿住空忍</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>nor in inner feelings of
emptiness.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一種平懷</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Be serene in the oneness of
things</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">泯然自盡</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and such erroneous views will
disappear by themselves.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">止動歸止</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When you try to stop activity to
achieve passivity</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">止更彌動</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>your very effort fills you with
activity.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">唯滯兩邊</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>As long as you remain in one extreme
or the other</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">寧知一種</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>you will never know Oneness.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一種不通</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Those who do not live in the single
Way</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">兩處失功</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>fail in both activity and
passivity,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">遣有沒有</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>assertion and denial. To deny the
reality of things</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">從空背空</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>to assert the emptiness of things is
to miss their reality.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">多言多慮</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The more you talk and think about
it,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">轉不相應</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>the further astray you wander from
the truth.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">絶言絶慮</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Stop talking and thinking,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無處不通</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and there is nothing you will not be
able to know.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">歸根得旨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>To return to the root is to find the
meaning,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">隨照失宗</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>but to pursue appearances is to miss
the source.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">須臾返照</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>At the moment of inner
enlightenment</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">勝卻前空</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> <span
style="mso-spacerun: yes"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">there is a going beyond
appearance and emptiness.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">前空轉變</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The changes that appear to occur in
the empty world</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">皆由妄見</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>we call real only because of our
ignorance.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不用求眞</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Do not search for the truth;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">唯須息見</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>only cease to cherish
opinions.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">二見不住</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Do not remain in the dualistic
state</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">慎莫追尋</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>avoid such pursuits carefully.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">纔有是非</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>If there is even a trace of this and
that, of right and wrong,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">紛然失心</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>the Mind-essence will be lost in
confusion.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">二由一有</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Although all dualities come from the
One,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一亦莫守</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>do not be attached even to this
One.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一心不生</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When the mind exists undisturbed in
the Way,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">萬法無咎</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>nothing in the world can
offend,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無咎無法</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and when a thing can no longer
offend, it ceases to exist in the old way.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不生不心</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When no discriminating thoughts
arise, the old mind ceases to exist.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">能隨境滅</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When thought objects vanish, the
thinking-subject vanishes,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">境逐能沈</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>as when the mind vanishes, objects
vanish.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">境由能境</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Things are objects because of the
subject (mind);</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">能由境能</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>the mind (subject) is such because of
things (object).</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">欲知兩段</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Understand the relativity of these
two</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">元是一空</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and the basic reality: the unity of
emptiness.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一空同兩</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>In this Emptiness the two are
indistinguishable</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">齊含萬象</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and each contains in itself the whole
world.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不見精</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">麁</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>If you do not discriminate between
coarse and fine</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">寧有偏黨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>you will not be tempted to prejudice
and opinion.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">大道體寛</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>To live in the Great Way</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無易無難</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>is neither easy nor difficult,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">小見狐疑</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>but those with limited views</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">轉急轉遲</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and fearful and irresolute: the
faster they hurry, the slower they go,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">執之失度</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and clinging (attachment) cannot be
limited;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">必<span
style="color:black">入邪路</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>even to be attached to the idea of
enlightenment is to go astray.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">放之自然</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Just let things be in their own
way</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">體無去住</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and there will be neither coming nor
going.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">任性合道</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Obey the nature of things (your own
nature),</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">逍遙絶惱</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and you will walk freely and
undisturbed.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">繋念乖眞</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When thought is in bondage the truth
is hidden,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">昏沈不好</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>for everything is murky and
unclear,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不好勞神</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and the burdensome practice of
judging brings annoyance and weariness.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">何用疏親</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>What benefit can be derived from
distinctions and separations?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">欲取一乘</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>If you wish to move in the One
Way</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">勿惡六塵</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>do not dislike even the world of
senses and ideas.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">六塵不惡</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Indeed, to accept them fully</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">還同正覺</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>is identical with true
Enlightenment.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">智者無爲</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>The wise man strives to no
goals</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">愚人自縛</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>but the foolish man fetters
himself.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">法無異法</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>This is one Dharma, not many:
distinctions arise</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">妄</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">自愛著</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span>from the clinging needs of the
ignorant.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">將心用心</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>To seek Mind with the
(discriminating) mind</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">豈非大錯</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>is the greatest of all
mistakes.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">迷生寂亂</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Rest and unrest derive from
illusion;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">悟無好惡</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>with enlightenment there is no liking
and disliking.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一切二邊</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>All dualities come from</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">妄</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">自斟酌</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span>ignorant inference.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">夢幻虚華</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>They are like dreams of flowers in
the air:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">何勞把捉</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>foolish to try to grasp them.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">得失是非</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Gain and loss, right and
wrong:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一時放卻</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>such thoughts must finally be
abolished at once.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">眼若不睡</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>If the eye never sleeps,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">諸夢</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">自除</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">   </span>all dreams will naturally
cease.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">心若不異</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>If the mind makes no
discriminations,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">萬法一如</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>the ten thousand things are as they
are, of single essence.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一如體玄</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>To understand the mystery of this
One-essence</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">兀爾忘虚</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>is to be release from all
entanglements.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">萬法齊觀</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When all things are seen
equally</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">歸復自然</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>the timeless Self-essence is
reached.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">泯其所以</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>No comparisons or analogies are
possible</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不可方比</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>in this causeless, relationless
state.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">止動無動</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Consider movement stationary and the
stationary in motion,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">動止無止</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>both movement and rest
disappear.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">兩既不成</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>When such dualities cease to
exist</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一何有爾</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Oneness itself cannot exist.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">究竟窮極</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>To this ultimate finality</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不存軌則</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>no law or description applies.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">契心平等</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>For the unified mind in accord with
the Way</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">所作倶息</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>all self-centered straining
ceases.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">狐疑盡淨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Doubts and irresolution's
vanish</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">正信調直</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and life in true faith is
possible.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一切不留</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>With a single stroke we are freed
from bondage;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無可記憶</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>nothing clings to us and we hold to
nothing.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">虚明自照</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>All is empty , clear,
self-illuminating,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不勞心力</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>with no exertion of the mind's
power.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">非思量處</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Here thought, feeling, knowledge, and
imagination</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">識情難測</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>are of no value.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">眞如法界</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>In this world of Suchness</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無他無自</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>there is neither self nor
other-than-self</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">要急相應</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>To come directly into harmony with
this reality</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">唯言不二</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>just simply say when doubt arises,
'Not two.'</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不二皆同</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>In this 'no two' nothing is
separate,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無不包容</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>nothing excluded.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">十方智者</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>No matter when or where,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">皆入此宗</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>enlightenment means entering this
truth.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">宗非促延</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>And this truth is beyond extension or
diminution in time or space;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一念萬年</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>in it a single thought is ten
thousand years.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無在不在</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Emptiness here, Emptiness
there,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">十方目前</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>but the infinite universe stands
always before your eyes.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">極小同大</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Infinitely large and infinitely
small;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">忘絶境界</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>no difference, for definitions have
vanished</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">極大同小</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不見邊表</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and no boundaries are seen.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">有即是無</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>So too with Being</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">無即是有</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>and non-Being.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">若不如此</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Don't waste time in doubts and
arguments</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">必不相守</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>that have nothing to do with
this.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一即一切</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>One thing, all things:</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">一切即一</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>move among and intermingle, without
distinction.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">但能如是</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>To live in this realization</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">何慮不畢</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>is to be without anxiety about
non-perfection.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">信心不二</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>To live in this faith is the road to
non-duality,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不二信心</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Because the non-dual is one with the
trusting mind.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">言語道斷</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Words! The Way is beyond
language,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">非去來今</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>for in it there is</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:3">                           </span>no
yesterday</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:3">                           </span>no
tomorrow</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:3">                           </span>no
today.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Another
Verse Attributed to *Chien-chih Seng-ts'an***</span><span
style="font-size:
16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Another
poetical composition attributed to *Chien-chih Seng-ts'an*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> is
found in *The Masters and Disciples of the Lanka*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (*Leng‑chia Shih-tzu
Chi*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, <span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">*Ryõga Shijiki*</span>). This is a poem
on "The Mysterious."</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*One Reality only –*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*How deep and far-reaching!*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*The ten thousand things –*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*How confusingly multifarious!*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*The true and the conventional are indeed
intermingling,*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*But essentially of the same substance they
are.*</span><span style="font-size:
13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*The wise and the unenlightened are indeed
distinguishable,*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*But in the Way they are united as
one.*</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*Desirest thou to find its limits?*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*How broadly expanding! It is
limitless!*</span><span style="font-size:13.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*How vaguely it vanishes away! Its ends are never
reached!*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>*It originates in beginningless time, it
terminates in endless time.*</span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>Translated by D.T. Suzuki (*Manual of Zen
Buddhism*</span><span style="font-size:
13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">)</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**A
Note on the Chinese Characters Used in the Texts**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Three
Chinese ideograms used in the article are incorrect. Due to problems
with encoding systems, they are replaced with similar ideograms. The
correct forms are given here using both traditional Chinese encoding
system (Big-5, Unicode) and pictures. The text in The Original Text
section is entirely correct, there are no false or replacement
characters.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**1.**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Stanza
13 line 1 ideogram 8<span style="mso-tab-count:2">          
</span>correct ideogram<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  
</span></span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">沉</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt"><img src="FaithMind_files/image014.jpg" width="20" height="20" /></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">能隨境滅、境逐能</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">沈</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
subject follows when the object ceases, the object is expelled when the
subject <span style="color:gray">sinks</span>.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**2.**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Stanza
15 line 1 ideogram 4<span style="mso-tab-count:2">          
</span>correct ideogram<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  
</span></span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">麤</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt"><sub><img src="FaithMind_files/image015.jpg" width="22" height="24" /></sub></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">不見精</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray">麁</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA">、寧有偏黨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Do not
differentiate <span style="color:gray">coarse</span> and fine, and you
will not be for or against.</span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**3.**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Stanza
18 line 1 ideogram 5<span style="mso-tab-count:2">          
</span>correct ideogram<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  
</span></span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">沉</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt"><img src="FaithMind_files/image016.jpg" width="20" height="20" /></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
2">                  </span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"> 
</span><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">        </span>ideogram 1<span style="mso-tab-count:2">         
</span> </span><span
style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">correct ideogram<span
style="mso-spacerun:
yes">   </span></span><span
style="font-size:2.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes"> </span></span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">繫</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">               </span></span><span
style="font-size:6.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW"><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes"> </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt"><img src="FaithMind_files/image018.jpg" width="21" height="21" /></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;mso-fareast-language:
JA">繋</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">念乖眞、昏</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:gray;
mso-fareast-language:JA">沈</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">不好</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:gray">Fettered</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
thinking strays from the real, it darkens, <span
style="color:gray">sinks</span> and spoils.<span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**4.**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
"Ts'an" of Seng-ts'an<span style="mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
3">                    </span></span>ideogram</span><span
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
2">                  </span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
